- [Low-Rank Matrix Recovery](/ai-engineering/low-rank-matrix-recovery.md) — concept · draft · nuclear norm as rank surrogate; matrix RIP; stable recovery; matrix completion (Netflix problem); Robust PCA (PCP)

- [Neural Tangent Kernel](/ai-engineering/neural-tangent-kernel.md) — concept · draft · infinite-width limit of deep networks; NTK fixed at initialization; gradient descent = kernel regression; depth/width as computation/statistical resources; manifold classification
